<Date>1428804146800</Date><UserId.>109744811928433206378< /UserId.>< Review>
3/10/15

I've been coming to this RT since my sister and I were little kids. We used to play on the Simpsons arcade machine at the front of the place before they remodeled it years ago. When my sister died unexpectedly a couple of weeks ago, my co-workers helped out my family by bringing homemade dinner to my parents and family every night of the week. The night before the funeral they ordered a Large and X-Large pizza for delivery to my parent's home, a mile away from this location. A special request to make heart-shaped pizza was included on the online order, and the pizzas were customized to end up with one meat and one veggie.

I received a call around 5 pm from RT - I had nothing to do with the ordering, as I'd been with my family all day handling funeral prep. They let me know that they weren't currently making the heart-shaped pizzas, and that pizza would arrive in about 40 minutes. However, it had been requested by the office that the pizzas be delivered at 6:40, so at 5:40 I was home wondering where the pizza was. I called RT back around 6 and asked what was going on - I was told that the person on the phone hadn't looked at the entire order, so I'd been waiting around for nothing. Everyone was really happy when the doorbell rang at 6:40.

My husband asked the driver if he'd already been tipped. He replied "well, sort of". We looked at the receipt. He received $5 to drive ONE MILE. It's a yes or no question. Sort of? What? Do you need more money for a 2 pizza delivery or are you just trying to trick a grieving family? We THEN saw that it was $98 (yes, NINETY EIGHT US DOLLARS) for the 2 pizzas. I called the manager, insisting there must be some mistake. But I was told by the supervisor on duty that customized pizzas are pretty expensive. I asked if there was anything she could do - these weren't very special pizzas. And their L/XL aren't very big. NOPE. That was it.

The girl in my office meant well by ordering something we'd like, but should have started with a veggie pizza and added toppings, rather than taking off and customizing, etc. Also, she thought she was getting heart-shaped pizza. Her heart was in the right place; and Round Table has no heart. They are just another greedy restaurant chain who lost someone as a customer who had so many fond memories after being a loyal fan for decades.< /Review>

<rating>5< /rating><Text>Dr. Wong is the first chiropractor I have seen.  What lead me to him was a mobility problem with my right shoulder and arm that was growing worse over the years.  I could no longer pull off my top because it hurt so much to make that over and up motion.  Eventually my arm started to go numb at night, and then ultimately I experienced numbness periodically throughout the day.  It was time to do something, but what?

According to my general practitioner, I needed to see a rheumatologist.  According to the rheumatologist, there was nothing wrong that needed fixing.  Perhaps it was my rotator cuff that was stressed but she couldn't tell from the x-rays.  She suggested that I do physical therapy, which I did, but this did not resolve the problem.  I modified my exercise routine and I set up my workspace to be more ergonomical.  Still no relief.

At the YMCA after a workout I saw that Greater Health Chiropractic was offering free chiropractic consultations, along with a 10 minute chair massage, which was excellent.  They also offered a free 30 minute massage if I came for a consultation.  I went for it.

I had my consultation and looked over the results with Dr. Wong that next week.  He described a plan of treatment and we got started that very day.  My first adjustment brought immediate mobility to my shoulder.  I was shocked.  Subsequent adjustments have focused on other areas of my spine that are in need to alignment, though not causing the sort of discomfort that my shoulder has.  The main issue is my neck, so every visit includes adjustments to my neck vertebrae plus I have started doing stretches that Dr. Wong showed me to my daily routine, which help a lot.  Also I've modified my sleeping habits (to sleep on my back) per Dr. Won't suggestion, and this helps too.

Taking a holistic approach to my body's health is making a bigger difference than the Western medical approach of isolating problems into specialties.  Adding acupuncture and massages to my chiropractic treatments will further help me, and I will do this when I can afford to do so.  It is frustrating that holistic medicine is not covered by my healthcare insurance!

I've been impressed by many things about this practice, including: Dr. Wong's professionalism and patience; the staff's friendliness and attention to detail; the free education seminars offered on various topics.  I would recommend Greater Life Chiropractic to others, who, like me, have relied on Western medicine to define our health treatment.  At least go for an initial consultation.  I'm very glad I did!<//Text><pics>None</pics>< resp>

We worked hard to satisfy your request although we had very, very, limited time to collect, to fill out, and to process, all of the necessary documents for providing moving services in the state of California. On August 15th you made a request to change your moving date to August 22nd, this forced us to send you an updated agreement in the form of email correspondence and phone call in order to notify you and confirm your moving date. This process generally takes up to 10 emails when the customer is unsure of the move date and not familiar with the detailed information they must provide to us about parking and packing and moving services. The responsibilities of a moving company (carrier) and the responsibilities of a client (shipper) generally assume the bulk of communications between the two parties prior to the move date. In conclusion, we definitely would like to apologize if our contact effort with you over-exceeded your expectations. Please let us know if you have any questions or concerns, and feel free to contact us by email or phone anytime.'}</resp>< Gmap_id>

<username>Faina Avrutina<//username><user>117572757794067061103</user>< review>
We had used All In Moving last week for two moves during our relocation process. We bought a new home and had to store some of our items in their storage while moving the rest to an apartment which we have rented until our new home is ready. They were terrific!  We had three different crews for three days, and each group was very professional, friendly and helpful.  Couple things I'd mention.  First, they were great at communication -- before and during each move.  I always felt confident that things were going as planned.  Second, they were incredibly resourceful.  We had a situation where there was a very narrow, windy staircase.  I was sure that we would not be able to get a large sofa into a 3rd floor apartment.  Sure enough, there was no way to get the sofa up the staircase.  Instead, they called two more of their crew to come (with my permission of course) and hoisted the sofa up outside the building (3 stories) and over the balcony into the living room!  Couldn't believe it and am so happy to have the sofa in the apartment.  Lastly, just want to reiterate our friendly and professional everyone was.  They constantly were moving pieces around as we were deciding where to put things.  In some cases, we moved a piece of furniture multiple times before settling on where we wanted it.  They did so without ever seeming to be put out.
We will be definitely be using All In for our next move, likely early next month.  Would HIGHLY recommend them!</review>
